          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            The Typescript enum seems a natural match with Angular2's ngSwitch directive.  But when I try to use an enum in my component's template, I get "Cannot read property 'xxx' of undefined in ...".  How can I use enum values in my component template?
           </p>
           <p>
            Please note that this is different from how to create html select options based upon ALL of the values of an enum (ngFor).  This question is about ngSwitch based upon a particular value of an enum.  Although the same approach of creating an class-internal reference to the enum appears.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="mt24 mb12">
           <div class="post-taglist d-flex gs4 gsy fd-column">
            <div class="d-flex ps-relative fw-wrap">
             <a class="post-tag" href="/questions/tagged/typescript" rel="tag" title="show questions tagged 'typescript'">
              typescript
             </a>
             <a class="post-tag" href="/questions/tagged/angular" rel="tag" title="show questions tagged 'angular'">
              angular
             </a>
            </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="35835985">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            </div>

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/35835985/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You can create a reference to the enum in your component class (I just changed the initial character to be lower-case) and then use that reference from the template (
             <a href="http://plnkr.co/edit/IY8R6qOwcgbLrXeBliFw?p=preview">
              plunker
             </a>
             ):
            </p>
            <pre><code>import {Component} from 'angular2/core';

enum CellType {Text, Placeholder}
class Cell {
  constructor(public text: string, public type: CellType) {}
}
@Component({
  selector: 'my-app',
  template: `
    &lt;div [ngSwitch]="cell.type"&gt;
      &lt;div *ngSwitchCase="cellType.Text"&gt;
        {{cell.text}}
      &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;div *ngSwitchCase="cellType.Placeholder"&gt;
        Placeholder
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;button (click)="setType(cellType.Text)"&gt;Text&lt;/button&gt;
    &lt;button (click)="setType(cellType.Placeholder)"&gt;Placeholder&lt;/button&gt;
  `,
})
export default class AppComponent {

  // Store a reference to the enum
  cellType = CellType;
  public cell: Cell;

  constructor() {
    this.cell = new Cell("Hello", CellType.Text)
  }

  setType(type: CellType) {
    this.cell.type = type;
  }
}
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="49088570">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             This's simple and works like a charm :)
just declare your enum like this and you can use it on HTML template
            </p>
            <pre><code>  statusEnum: typeof StatusEnum = StatusEnum;
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="41730451" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="3" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="91" id="answer-41730451" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="41730451">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="91" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             91
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/41730451/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You can create a custom decorator to add to your component to make it aware of enums.
            </p>
            <h2>
             myenum.enum.ts:
            </h2>
            <pre><code>export enum MyEnum {
    FirstValue,
    SecondValue
}
</code></pre>
            <h2>
             myenumaware.decorator.ts
            </h2>
            <pre><code>import { MyEnum } from './myenum.enum';

export function MyEnumAware(constructor: Function) {
    constructor.prototype.MyEnum = MyEnum;
}
</code></pre>
            <h2>
             enum-aware.component.ts
            </h2>
            <pre><code>import { Component } from '@angular2/core';
import { MyEnum } from './myenum.enum';
import { MyEnumAware } from './myenumaware.decorator';

@Component({
  selector: 'enum-aware',
  template: `
    &lt;div [ngSwitch]="myEnumValue"&gt;
      &lt;div *ngSwitchCase="MyEnum.FirstValue"&gt;
        First Value
      &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;div *ngSwitchCase="MyEnum.SecondValue"&gt;
        Second Value
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;button (click)="toggleValue()"&gt;Toggle Value&lt;/button&gt;
  `,
})
@MyEnumAware // &lt;---------------!!!
export default class EnumAwareComponent {
  myEnumValue: MyEnum = MyEnum.FirstValue;

  toggleValue() {
    this.myEnumValue = this.myEnumValue === MyEnum.FirstValue
        ? MyEnum.SecondValue : MyEnum.FirstValue;
  }
}
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="76405678" data-comment-owner-id="4342563" data-comment-score="2" id="comment-76405678">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @Simon_Weaver
                 <b>
                  decorators
                 </b>
                 are essentially functions that take a function as a parameter and extend the behavior of that function.  In the case of ES6/7, we're dealing with the extension/annotation of classes.  Here's a
                 <a href="https://medium.com/google-developers/exploring-es7-decorators-76ecb65fb841" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  high level article about how they work
                 </a>
                 .  The
                 <a href="https://tc39.github.io/proposal-decorators/#sec-intro" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  proposal for implementation in ES7
                 </a>
                 is on github - currently in stage 2.  In that proposal, they touch on possible uses for decorators.  TypeScript, being a superset of JS, includes this feature.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/4342563/eric-lease" title="4,024 reputation">
                  Eric Lease
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2017-06-23 00:57:10Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Jun 23, 2017 at 0:57
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="76405797" data-comment-owner-id="4342563" data-comment-score="2" id="comment-76405797">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 2
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @Simon_Weaver In this case, the syntactic sugar is hiding the call to
                 <code>
                  MyEnumAware()
                 </code>
                 , where the
                 <code>
                  EnumAwareComponent
                 </code>
                 instance is passed, and has a property,
                 <code>
                  MyEnum
                 </code>
                 , added to its prototype.  The value of the property is set the enum itself.  This method does the same thing as the accepted answer.  It's just taking advantage of the syntactic sugar proposed for decorators and allowed in TypeScript.  When using Angular you're using decorator syntax right off the bat.  That's what a
                 <code>
                  Component
                 </code>
                 <i>
                  is
                 </i>
                 , an extension of an empty class that Angular's core classes know how to interact with.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/4342563/eric-lease" title="4,024 reputation">
                  Eric Lease
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2017-06-23 01:08:17Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Jun 23, 2017 at 1:08
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span title="this comment was edited 1 time">
                 <svg aria-hidden="true" class="va-text-bottom o50 svg-icon iconPencilSm" height="14" viewbox="0 0 14 14" width="14">
                  <path d="m11.1 1.71 1.13 1.12c.2.2.2.51 0 .71L11.1 4.7 9.21 2.86l1.17-1.15c.2-.2.51-.2.71 0ZM2 10.12l6.37-6.43 1.88 1.88L3.88 12H2v-1.88Z">
                  </path>
                 </svg>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="77617564" data-comment-owner-id="183406" data-comment-score="5" id="comment-77617564">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">

                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 -1: This does not appear to work with aot, resulting in
                 <code>
                  ERROR in ng:///.../whatever.component.html (13,3): Property 'MyEnum' does not exist on type 'EnumAwareComponent'
                 </code>
                 . This makes sense, because the property the decorator adds is never declared, leaving the typescript compiler unaware of its existence.
                </span>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Angular4 - Using Enum in HTML Template  ngSwitch / ngSwitchCase
            </p>
            <p>
             Solution here:
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/42464835/802196">
              https://stackoverflow.com/a/42464835/802196
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             credit: @snorkpete
            </p>
            <p>
             In your component, you have
            </p>
            <pre><code>enum MyEnum{
  First,
  Second
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Then in your component, you bring in the Enum type via a member 'MyEnum', and create another member for your enum variable 'myEnumVar' :
            </p>
            <pre><code>export class MyComponent{
  MyEnum = MyEnum;
  myEnumVar:MyEnum = MyEnum.Second
  ...
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             You can now use myEnumVar and MyEnum in your .html template.  Eg, Using Enums in ngSwitch:
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;div [ngSwitch]="myEnumVar"&gt;
  &lt;div *ngSwitchCase="MyEnum.First"&gt;&lt;app-first-component&gt;&lt;/app-first-component&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;div *ngSwitchCase="MyEnum.Second"&gt;&lt;app-second-component&gt;&lt;/app-second-component&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;div *ngSwitchDefault&gt;MyEnumVar {{myEnumVar}} is not handled.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             as of rc.6 / final
            </p>
            <p>
             ...
            </p>
            <pre><code>export enum AdnetNetworkPropSelector {
    CONTENT,
    PACKAGE,
    RESOURCE
}

&lt;div style="height: 100%"&gt;
          &lt;div [ngSwitch]="propSelector"&gt;
                 &lt;div *ngSwitchCase="adnetNetworkPropSelector.CONTENT"&gt;
                      &lt;AdnetNetworkPackageContentProps [setAdnetContentModels]="adnetNetworkPackageContent.selectedAdnetContentModel"&gt;
                                    &lt;/AdnetNetworkPackageContentProps&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                 &lt;div *ngSwitchCase="adnetNetworkPropSelector.PACKAGE"&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;              
        &lt;/div&gt;


export class AdnetNetwork {       
    private adnetNetworkPropSelector = AdnetNetworkPropSelector;
    private propSelector = AdnetNetworkPropSelector.CONTENT;
}
</code></pre>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="51307059" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="6" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="17" id="answer-51307059" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="51307059">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="17" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             17
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/51307059/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             As an alternative to @Eric Lease's decorator, which unfortunately doesn't work using
             <code>
              --aot
             </code>
             (and thus
             <code>
              --prod
             </code>
             ) builds, I resorted to using a service which exposes all my application's enums. Just need to publicly inject that into each component which requires it, under an easy name, after which you can access the enums in your views. E.g.:
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Service
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>import { Injectable } from '@angular/core';
import { MyEnumType } from './app.enums';

@Injectable()
export class EnumsService {
  MyEnumType = MyEnumType;
  // ...
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Don't forget to include it in your module's provider list.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Component class
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>export class MyComponent {
  constructor(public enums: EnumsService) {}
  @Input() public someProperty: MyEnumType;

  // ...
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Component html
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;div *ngIf="someProperty === enums.MyEnumType.SomeValue"&gt;Match!&lt;/div&gt;
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <a name="51313765">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="51313765" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="2" id="answer-51313765" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="51313765">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="2" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             2
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/51313765/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <h3>
             Start by considering 'Do I
             <em>
              really
             </em>
             want to do this?'
            </h3>
            <p>
             I have no problem referring to enums directly in HTML, but in some cases there are cleaner alternatives that don't lose type-safe-ness.
For instance if you choose the approach shown in my other answer, you may have declared TT in your component something like this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>public TT = 
{
    // Enum defines (Horizontal | Vertical)
    FeatureBoxResponsiveLayout: FeatureBoxResponsiveLayout   
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             To show a different layout in your HTML, you'd have an
             <code>
              *ngIf
             </code>
             for each layout type, and you could refer directly to the enum in your component's HTML:
            </p>
            <pre><code>*ngIf="(featureBoxResponsiveService.layout | async) == TT.FeatureBoxResponsiveLayout.Horizontal"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This example uses a service to get the current layout, runs it through the async pipe and then compares it to our enum value. It's pretty verbose, convoluted and not much fun to look at. It also exposes the name of the enum, which itself may be overly verbose.
            </p>
            <h3>
             Alternative, that retains type safety from the HTML
            </h3>
            <p>
             Alternatively you can do the following, and declare a more readable function in your component's .ts file :
            </p>
            <pre><code>*ngIf="isResponsiveLayout('Horizontal')"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Much cleaner! But what if someone types in
             <code>
              'Horziontal'
             </code>
             by mistake? The whole reason you wanted to use an enum in the HTML was to be typesafe right?
            </p>
            <p>
             We can still achieve that with
             <a href="https://www.typescriptlang.org/docs/handbook/release-notes/typescript-2-9.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              keyof
             </a>
             and some typescript magic. This is the definition of the function:
            </p>
            <pre><code>isResponsiveLayout(value: keyof typeof FeatureBoxResponsiveLayout)
{
    return FeatureBoxResponsiveLayout[value] == this.featureBoxResponsiveService.layout.value;
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Note the usage of
             <code>
              FeatureBoxResponsiveLayout[string]
             </code>
             which
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/17380845/how-to-convert-string-to-enum-in-typescript">
              converts
             </a>
             the string value passed in to the numeric value of the enum.
            </p>
            <p>
             This will give an error message with an AOT compilation if you use an invalid value.
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              Argument of type '"H4orizontal"' is not assignable to parameter of type '"Vertical" | "Horizontal"
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             Currently VSCode isn't smart enough to underline
             <code>
              H4orizontal
             </code>
             in the HTML editor, but you'll get the warning at compile time (with --prod build or --aot switch). This also may be improved upon in a future update.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2018-07-12T20:15:34" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="51313765">
               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">
                <div class="flex--item">
                 <a class="js-share-link js-gps-track" data-controller="se-share-sheet" data-gps-track="post.click({ item: 2, priv: 0, post_type: 2 })" data-s-popover-placement="bottom-start" data-se-share-sheet-license-name="CC BY-SA 4.0" data-se-share-sheet-license-url="https%3a%2f%2fcreativecommons.org%2flicenses%2fby-sa%2f4.0%2f" data-se-share-sheet-location="2" data-se-share-sheet-post-type="answer" data-se-share-sheet-social="facebook twitter devto" data-se-share-sheet-subtitle="" data-se-share-sheet-title="Share a link to this answer" href="/a/51313765" itemprop="url" rel="nofollow" title="Short permalink to this answer">
                  Share
                 </a>
                </div>
                <div class="flex--item">
                 <a class="js-suggest-edit-post js-gps-track" data-gps-track="post.click({ item: 6, priv: 0, post_type: 2 })" href="/posts/51313765/edit" title="">
                  Improve this answer
                 </a>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="55731812" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="8" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="2" id="answer-55731812" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="55731812">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="2" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             2
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/55731812/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             My component used an object
             <code>
              myClassObject
             </code>
             of type
             <code>
              MyClass
             </code>
             , which itself was using
             <code>
              MyEnum
             </code>
             . This lead to the same issue described above. Solved it by doing:
            </p>
            <pre><code>export enum MyEnum {
    Option1,
    Option2,
    Option3
}
export class MyClass {
    myEnum: typeof MyEnum;
    myEnumField: MyEnum;
    someOtherField: string;
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             and then using this in the template as
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;div [ngSwitch]="myClassObject.myEnumField"&gt;
  &lt;div *ngSwitchCase="myClassObject.myEnum.Option1"&gt;
    Do something for Option1
  &lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;div *ngSwitchCase="myClassObject.myEnum.Option2"&gt;
    Do something for Option2
  &lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;div *ngSwitchCase="myClassObject.myEnum.Option3"&gt;
    Do something for Opiton3
  &lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <a name="44662893">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="44662893" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="9" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1" id="answer-44662893" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="44662893">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/44662893/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If using the 'typetable reference' approach (from @Carl G) and you're using multiple type tables you might want to consider this way :
            </p>
            <pre><code>export default class AppComponent {

  // Store a reference to the enums (must be public for --AOT to work)
  public TT = { 
       CellType: CellType, 
       CatType: CatType, 
       DogType: DogType 
  };

  ...

  dog = DogType.GoldenRetriever; 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Then access in your html file with
            </p>
            <pre><code>{{ TT.DogType[dog] }}   =&gt; "GoldenRetriever"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             I favor this approach as it makes it clear you're referring to a typetable, and also avoids unnecessary pollution of your component file.
            </p>
            <p>
             You can also put a global
             <code>
              TT
             </code>
             somewhere and add enums to it as needed (if you want this you may as well make a service as shown by @VincentSels answer). If you have many many typetables this may become cumbersome.
            </p>
            <p>
             Also you always rename them in your declaration to get a shorter name.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2017-06-20T20:59:19" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

                 </a>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="70027671" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="10" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="0" id="answer-70027671" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="70027671">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="0" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             0
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/70027671/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You can now do this:
            </p>
            <p>
             for example, the enum is:
            </p>
            <pre><code>export enum MessagePriority {
    REGULAR= 1,
    WARNING,
    IMPORTANT,
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             a status message, that looks like this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>export default class StatusMessage{
    message: string;
    priority: MessagePriority;

    constructor(message: string, priority: MessagePriority){
        this.message = message;
        this.priority = priority;
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             then in the .ts file of the component you can do this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>    import StatusMessage from '../../src/entities/building/ranch/administration/statusMessage';
    import { MessagePriority } from '../../enums/message-priority';
            
    export class InfoCardComponent implements OnInit {
     messagePriority: typeof MessagePriority;
                
     constructor() { 
     this.messagePriority = MessagePriority;
    }
                
    @Input() statusMessage: StatusMessage;
    ngOnInit(): void {}
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             and finally the HTML of the component looks like this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;div class="info-card" [ngSwitch]="statusMessage.priority"&gt;
    &lt;h2 *ngSwitchCase="this.messagePriority.REGULAR" class="info-card__regular-message"&gt;{{statusMessage.message}}&lt;/h2&gt;
    &lt;h2 *ngSwitchCase="this.messagePriority.WARNING" class="info-card__warning-message"&gt;{{statusMessage.message}}&lt;/h2&gt;
    &lt;h2 *ngSwitchCase="this.messagePriority.IMPORTANT" class="info-card__important-message"&gt;{{statusMessage.message}}&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Notice that the enum is first declared to the class with the type of "typeof MessagePriority", then bound to the class by calling the definition with "this.messagePriority = MessagePriority"
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
